position.coords.latitude + \"\\nlng = \" + position.coords.longitude);\n    };\n\n    var browserGeolocationFail = function(error) {\n       switch (error.code) {\n           case error.TIMEOUT:\n    //               alert(\"Browser geolocation error !\\n\\nTimeout.\");\n               break;\n           case error.PERMISSION_DENIED:\n               if(error.message.indexOf(\"Only secure origins are allowed\") == 0) {\n                   tryAPIGeolocation();\n               }\n               break;\n           case error.POSITION_UNAVAILABLE:\n    //               alert(\"Browser geolocation error !\\n\\nPosition unavailable.\");\n               break;\n       }\n    };\n\n    var tryGeolocation = function() {\n\n       var res=confirm(\"Would you like to share your location with this  site!\");\n       if(res){\n           var iscomingfirsttimeValue= 1;\n           setCookie(\"iscomingfirsttime\", iscomingfirsttimeValue, 1);\n           if (navigator.geolocation) {\n               navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(\n                   browserGeolocationSuccess,\n                   browserGeolocationFail,\n                   {maximumAge: 50000, timeout: 20000, enableHighAccuracy: true});\n           }\n           $.ajax({\n               type: \"POST\",\n               url: '/pages/landingPageEvents',\n               data: {'Isacceptd':1},\n               success: function(data) {\n                   $('.upcomingEventData').html(data);\n                   owlCarouselInit(\"#owl-demo\");\n               }\n           });\n       }else{\n           var iscomingfirsttimeValue= 2;\n           setCookie(\"iscomingfirsttime\", iscomingfirsttimeValue, 1);\n           $.ajax({\n               type: \"POST\",\n               url: '/pages/landingPageEvents',\n               data: {'Isacceptd':2},\n               success: function(data) {\n                   $('.upcomingEventData').html(data);\n                   owlCarouselInit(\"#owl-demo\");\n               }\n           });\n       }\n    };\n\n    var postLocation=function(lat,lng){\n\n       var iscomingfirsttimeValue= 1;\n       setCookie(\"iscomingfirsttime\", iscomingfirsttimeValue, 1);\n       $.ajax({\n           type: \"POST\",\n           url: '/pages/landingPageEvents',\n           data: {'Isacceptd':1,'lat':lat,'lng':lng},\n           success: function(data) {\n               $('.upcomingEventData').html(data);\n               owlCarouselInit(\"#owl-demo\");\n           }\n       });\n    }\n\n    $(document).ready(function() {\n\n        var iscomingfirsttime=getCookie(\"iscomingfirsttime\");\n\n\n        if(iscomingfirsttime == \"\"){\n            tryGeolocation();\n        }\n        else{\n            if(iscomingfirsttime == 1){   // cookies set for share location\n                 $.ajax({\n                        type: \"POST\",\n                        url: '/pages/landingPageEvents',\n                        data: {'Isacceptd':1},\n                        success: function(data) {\n                                $('.upcomingEventData').html(data);\n function(data) {\n                                $('.upcomingEventData').html(data);\n                                owlCarouselInit(\"#owl-demo\");\n                        }\n                    });\n            }\n        }\n        $('#myCarousel3').carousel({\n            interval: 1000 * 06\n        });\n        $('.carousel-control.left').click(function() {\n
